Later, I turned on the air conditioner. At first, I didn't know it was broken. I blew it for a long time and there was no response. It was raining outside, and the room was very stuffy. The two children kept shouting that it was hot, so I called the front desk to ask. He told me that the air conditioner was short-circuited and broken because the children were already taking a shower in it. I thought I'd just make do with it. They gave us a small fan, but it was still very hot. I slept all night because it was hot and I didn't sleep well. I felt stuffy and lacked oxygen. The worst thing was that there was not even a washing machine. It was not as good as the Hanting Hotel in the small town. People all have washing machines and dryers.
